<script type="text/javascript">
	(function($) {
		var cache = {};
		
		$( "#item_search" ).autocomplete({
			minLength: 3,
			source: function( request, response ) {
				var term = request.term;
				if ( term in cache ) {
					response( cache[ term ] );
					return;
				}
				
				$.getJSON( "http://forums.zybez.net/index.php?app=priceguide&module=public&section=search", request, function( data, status, xhr ) {
					cache[ term ] = data;
					response( data );
				});
			},
			select: function( event, ui ) {
				window.location.href = ui.item.rel;
				ui.item.value = ui.item.label;
			},
			focus: function( event, ui ) {
				ui.item.value = ui.item.label;
			}
		}).data( "ui-autocomplete" )._renderItem = function( ul, item ) {
			if( typeof item.image != 'undefined' ) {
				return $( '<li>' )
					.append( '<a href="' + item.rel + '"><small class="right">' + item.price + '</small>' + '<img src="' + item.image + '" style="width:27px; height:27px; margin:-5px 0 -3px -4px;" /> ' + item.label + '</a>' )
					.appendTo( ul );
			}
			else if( typeof item.rel != 'undefined' ) {
				return $( '<li>' )
					.append( '<a href="' + item.rel + '">' + item.label + '</a>' )
					.appendTo( ul );
			}
			else {
				return $( '<li>' )
					.append( '<div class="ipsPad">' + item.label + '</div>' )
					.appendTo( ul );
			}
		};
		
		$( ".ipsLayout_content .message.success, .ipsLayout_content .message.error:not(.clickhide)" ).click(function() {
 			$(this).fadeOut();
		});
		
		$( ".clickhide" ).each(function() {
			if( ipb.Cookie.get( this.id ) != this.id ) {
				$(this).show();
			}
		});
		
		$( ".clickhide .right").click(function() {
			$(this).parent().fadeOut();
			ipb.Cookie.set( $(this).parent().attr('id'), $(this).parent().attr('id') );
 		});
	})(jQuery);
</script>

				jQuery(function () {
					if (jQuery(".t-footer-browse").length > 0) {
						jQuery(".t-footer-browse").delegate(".j-footer-item > a", "click", function (g) {
							g.preventDefault();
							var f = jQuery(this).closest(".t-footer-browse");
							f.find(".j-footer-item ul").removeClass("j-list-selected");
							f.find(".j-footer-item > a").removeClass("j-selected");
							jQuery(this).parent().find("ul").addClass("j-list-selected");
							jQuery(this).addClass("j-selected")
						})
					}
				});
				</script>
		</footer>
